<div id="review_409228108" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/409228108" />
    <a title="Catherine Fitzsimmons" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12614960-catherine-fitzsimmons"><img alt="Catherine Fitzsimmons" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1347028494p2/12614960.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/409228108?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catherine Fitzsimmons" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catherine Fitzsimmons" href="/user/show/12614960-catherine-fitzsimmons">Catherine Fitzsimmons</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer409228108" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4646264760409425198">A children’s novel by a debut author about a young queen who must make allies with mystical neighbors and lead her people into war with a massive and highly advanced invading army that seeks to destroy her country. I had high hopes for this book based on the synopsis, and given that it was in the adult clearance section of the bookstore, I didn’t realize it was a children’s book until I started reading it. It was alright for a children’s book, again entertaining, but nothing to write home about.</span>
  <span id="freeText4646264760409425198" style="display:none">A children’s novel by a debut author about a young queen who must make allies with mystical neighbors and lead her people into war with a massive and highly advanced invading army that seeks to destroy her country. I had high hopes for this book based on the synopsis, and given that it was in the adult clearance section of the bookstore, I didn’t realize it was a children’s book until I started reading it. It was alright for a children’s book, again entertaining, but nothing to write home about. The characters are pretty stereotypical and a little exaggerated, the conflict and story simplistic, and there’s no attempt made at adding any creative spin to the well-used concepts in the story. There are Vampires and Werewolves and such things, and you’re just supposed to take them at face value when there’s enough detail in the writing that there really should be more to them. It’s not a bad read, it’s just nothing special or original. Good to stave off boredom but hardly fulfilling if searching for an engaging or interesting book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4646264760409425198" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/750220552?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mackenzie Hendricks" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mackenzie Hendricks" href="/user/show/24033956-mackenzie-hendricks">Mackenzie Hendricks</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24033956-mackenzie-hendricks?shelf=yal-1-12">yal-1-12</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer750220552" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5754622940766722931">The first installment of the Icemark Chronicles by Stuart Hill is set in the fantasy land of the Icemark and follows 14-year-old Princess Thirrin Freer Strong-in-the-arm Lindenshield, Wildcat of the North. When the small land is threatened by the large, industrialized Polypontian Empire Thirrin seeks desperately to find allies to prevent her small land from being destroyed. Werewolves, vampires, witches, and much more exist in the lands around her, but convincing them to fight with her is a batt</span>
  <span id="freeText5754622940766722931" style="display:none">The first installment of the Icemark Chronicles by Stuart Hill is set in the fantasy land of the Icemark and follows 14-year-old Princess Thirrin Freer Strong-in-the-arm Lindenshield, Wildcat of the North. When the small land is threatened by the large, industrialized Polypontian Empire Thirrin seeks desperately to find allies to prevent her small land from being destroyed. Werewolves, vampires, witches, and much more exist in the lands around her, but convincing them to fight with her is a battle in itself. <br /><br />I loved this book. From the very first page you are engaged and excited by the fiery, brave protagonist, Thirrin, and the story only accelerates from there. Hill writes delightful fighting scenes with great detail, and he also carefully develops his characters. Although the story centers around the classic idea of David and Goliath, it also focuses on finding yourself and coming of age. I would highly recommend this book to others.<br /><br />Content issue: war and violence, nothing overly graphic.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1376255979" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1376255979" />
    <a title="Derrek Kemper" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/46373764-derrek-kemper"><img alt="Derrek Kemper" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1376255979?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Derrek Kemper" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Derrek Kemper" href="/user/show/46373764-derrek-kemper">Derrek Kemper</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1376255979" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5267424277288782416">I give "The Cry of the Icemark" a 10 out of 10. I give it this rating because throughout the book there is a interesting event happening so I just wanted to keep reading it and I couldn't stop sometimes. Also, I give it a 10 out of 10 because the characters in the book just flow right into the plot with the treat of war coming the new young queen Thirrin seeks out to find allies that with help them in the upcoming war between her and the General of the Polypontian Empire Scipio Bellorum. I would</span>
  <span id="freeText5267424277288782416" style="display:none">I give "The Cry of the Icemark" a 10 out of 10. I give it this rating because throughout the book there is a interesting event happening so I just wanted to keep reading it and I couldn't stop sometimes. Also, I give it a 10 out of 10 because the characters in the book just flow right into the plot with the treat of war coming the new young queen Thirrin seeks out to find allies that with help them in the upcoming war between her and the General of the Polypontian Empire Scipio Bellorum. I would recommend to people who like fantasy, adventure, and mystery. The audience that would most likely have the most interest in this book would be people that like young adult fiction, adventure, and suspense. In this book a 13 year old girl named Thirrin has is preparing to become queen of the Icemark and now she has. Now she has to find a way to protect the Icemark her kingdom from the invasion from General Scipio Bellorum. She will have to find allies with many different empires and learns a lot on the way. I guest you just have to read it to find out what happens.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5267424277288782416" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('yRzzfBAXtqMnopLXq3cGcnySOZ1hleeoD5JZssVQ30gl9TrnL3A77Fz60yZ+ql0on+hOOGdMKhQArGHZJfEkUA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('rBzZ3YaoSNSjRRc7ylrUrQ3t3A9Rj+fXcvQqQzNUNa5A9RBGuc/Fm9gdVsofh4/37perqldWKmt9yhIo0/XOtg==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer10164155786206244530">Stuart Hill was born in Leicester, in the East Midlands of England, where he still lives today. His family heritage includes English, Irish, Romany and Jewish blood. As a student his grades were average at best, but he was fortunate to have a teacher who inspired in him a lifelong love of reading. Since leaving school, he has worked as a teacher and an archaeologist, and now balances life as both </span>
  <span id="freeText10164155786206244530" style="display:none">Stuart Hill was born in Leicester, in the East Midlands of England, where he still lives today. His family heritage includes English, Irish, Romany and Jewish blood. As a student his grades were average at best, but he was fortunate to have a teacher who inspired in him a lifelong love of reading. Since leaving school, he has worked as a teacher and an archaeologist, and now balances life as both a bookseller and a writer. <br /><br />The Cry of the Icemark is his first novel. When he was a teenager, Stuart lost "the real Thirrin," his red-haired sister Kathleen, to leukemia. The story of the brave young warrior-queen who faces impossible dangers is dedicated to her. The Cry of the Icemark won the Ottakars Prize for the best new children’s novel - Ottakars is one of the UK's leading book chains. Foreign rights have been sold to over 14 countries, and Fox have bought the movie rights. <br /><br />Blade of Fire, the second in the Icemark Chronicles series was published in the UK in September 2006 and in the USA in February 2007. <br /><br />Stuart says that his influences include H. Rider Haggard, J.R.R. Tolkien, C.S. Lewis, and Margaret Abbey—his former grade school teacher who is also a writer of historical novels. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10164155786206244530" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
